DATABASE SPECIFICATION DOCUMENT (DSD)
I. GI???I THI???U
1.1. M???c ????ch t??i li???u
Database Specification Document ?????c t??? chi ti???t c???u tr??c v???t l?? c???a c?? s??? d??? li???u ???????c tri???n khai tr??n PostgreSQL . T??i li???u x??c ?????nh:
Danh s??ch b???ng v?? c???t d??? li???u.
Ki???u d??? li???u PostgreSQL .
Kh??a ch??nh, kh??a ngo???i v?? kh??a duy nh???t.
Gi?? tr??? m???c ?????nh v?? kh??? n??ng ????? tr???ng.
Mi???n gi?? tr??? v?? r??ng bu???c ki???m tra.
Ch??? m???c ph???c v??? t??m ki???m.
Transaction ph???c v??? c??c nghi???p v??? quan tr???ng.
Ch??nh s??ch x??a, b???o m???t, sao l??u v?? ph???c h???i.
Kh??? n??ng truy v???t t??? y??u c???u ?????n b???ng d??? li???u.
C???u tr??c c?? s??? d??? li???u ???????c suy di???n t??? BRD, SyRS, Static Model v?? Dynamic Model. Static Model x??c ?????nh 12 l???p <<entity>>, thu???c t??nh, quan h??? v?? b???i s???; Dynamic Model x??c ?????nh tr???ng th??i, quy t???c chuy???n tr???ng th??i v?? c??ch c???p nh???t d??? li???u trong t???ng nghi???p v???.
1.2. Ph???m vi
DSD bao ph??? d??? li???u c???a c??c nh??m ch???c n??ng:
SyRS x??c ?????nh h??? th???ng kh??ng bao g???m thanh to??n tr???c tuy???n, v???n chuy???n, theo d??i v??? tr?? th???i gian th???c v?? t??ch h???p h??? th???ng b??n ngo??i; v?? v???y DSD kh??ng thi???t k??? c??c b???ng cho nh???ng ch???c n??ng n??y.
1.3. T??i li???u tham kh???o
II. M??I TR?????NG V?? QUY ?????C TRI???N KHAI
2.1. C???u h??nh c?? s??? d??? li???u
PostgreSQL h??? tr??? ki???u d??? li???u BOOLEAN nguy??n b???n, ki???u UUID, d??? li???u JSON/JSONB v?? c??c ki???u ng??y gi??? c?? m??i gi???. Trong ph???m vi ????? ??n, kh??a ch??nh ???????c l??u b???ng ki???u UUID v?? ???????c sinh t??? ?????ng b???ng h??m gen_random_uuid() thu???c extension pgcrypto.
2.2. Kh???i t???o database
CREATE DATABASE asset_sharing 
WITH ENCODING = 'UTF8'; 
2.3. Quy t???c ?????t t??n
III. DANH S??CH B???NG D??? LI???U
M?????i hai b???ng d??? li???u ???????c chuy???n ?????i tr???c ti???p t??? 12 l???p <<entity>> ???? x??c ?????nh trong Static Model.
IV. ?????C T??? CHI TI???T C??C B???NG
4.1. B???ng nguoi_dung
CREATE TABLE nguoi_dung (
    nguoi_dung_id UUID NOT NULL DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    email VARCHAR(254),
    so_dien_thoai VARCHAR(20),
    mat_khau_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    vai_tro VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL
        DEFAULT 'THANH_VIEN',
    trang_thai VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL
        DEFAULT 'CHO_XAC_THUC',
    ngay_tao TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    ngay_cap_nhat TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT pk_nguoi_dung
        PRIMARY KEY (nguoi_dung_id),
    CONSTRAINT uq_nguoi_dung_email
        UNIQUE(email),
    CONSTRAINT uq_nguoi_dung_so_dien_thoai
        UNIQUE(so_dien_thoai),
    CONSTRAINT ck_nguoi_dung_dang_nhap
        CHECK(
            email IS NOT NULL
            OR so_dien_thoai IS NOT NULL
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_nguoi_dung_vai_tro
        CHECK(
            vai_tro IN(
                'THANH_VIEN',
                'QUAN_TRI_VIEN'
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_nguoi_dung_trang_thai
        CHECK(
            trang_thai IN(
                'CHO_XAC_THUC',
                'HOAT_DONG',
                'BI_KHOA',
                'NGUNG_HOAT_DONG'
            )
        )
);
4.2. B???ng ho_so_thanh_vien
CREATE TABLE ho_so_thanh_vien (
    ho_so_id UUID
        DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    nguoi_dung_id UUID NOT NULL,
    ho_ten VARCHAR(150) NOT NULL,
    anh_dai_dien VARCHAR(500),
    dia_chi VARCHAR(255),
    mo_ta_ca_nhan TEXT,
    ngay_cap_nhat TIMESTAMPTZ
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT pk_ho_so_thanh_vien
        PRIMARY KEY(ho_so_id),
    CONSTRAINT uq_ho_so_nguoi_dung
        UNIQUE(nguoi_dung_id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_ho_so_nguoi_dung
        FOREIGN KEY(nguoi_dung_id)
        REFERENCES nguoi_dung(nguoi_dung_id)
        ON DELETE RESTRICT
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
);
4.3. B???ng ho_so_uy_tin
CREATE TABLE ho_so_uy_tin (
    ho_so_uy_tin_id UUID
        DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    nguoi_dung_id UUID NOT NULL,
    diem_trung_binh NUMERIC(3,2)
        DEFAULT 0.00,
    tong_so_danh_gia INTEGER
        DEFAULT 0,
    so_giao_dich_hoan_tat INTEGER
        DEFAULT 0,
    ngay_cap_nhat TIMESTAMPTZ
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT pk_ho_so_uy_tin
        PRIMARY KEY(ho_so_uy_tin_id),
    CONSTRAINT uq_ho_so_uy_tin
        UNIQUE(nguoi_dung_id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_ho_so_uy_tin
        FOREIGN KEY(nguoi_dung_id)
        REFERENCES nguoi_dung(nguoi_dung_id),
    CONSTRAINT ck_diem_uy_tin
        CHECK(
            diem_trung_binh BETWEEN 0 AND 5
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_so_lieu_uy_tin
        CHECK(
            tong_so_danh_gia>=0
            AND so_giao_dich_hoan_tat>=0
        )
);
4.4. B???ng danh_muc_tai_san
CREATE TABLE danh_muc_tai_san(
    danh_muc_id UUID
        DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    ten_danh_muc VARCHAR(100)
        NOT NULL,
    mo_ta TEXT,
    trang_thai VARCHAR(30)
        DEFAULT 'HOAT_DONG',
    ngay_tao TIMESTAMPTZ
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT pk_danh_muc
        PRIMARY KEY(danh_muc_id),
    CONSTRAINT uq_ten_danh_muc
        UNIQUE(ten_danh_muc),
    CONSTRAINT ck_trang_thai_danh_muc
        CHECK(
            trang_thai IN(
                'HOAT_DONG',
                'NGUNG_SU_DUNG'
            )
        )
);
4.5. B???ng bai_dang_tai_san
CREATE TABLE bai_dang_tai_san(
    bai_dang_id UUID
        DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    chu_so_huu_id UUID NOT NULL,
    danh_muc_id UUID NOT NULL,
    ten_tai_san VARCHAR(200)
        NOT NULL,
    mo_ta_hien_trang TEXT
        NOT NULL,
    so_luong_tong INTEGER
        NOT NULL,
    so_luong_kha_dung INTEGER
        NOT NULL,
    so_luong_giu_cho INTEGER
        DEFAULT 0,
    so_luong_da_phan_phoi INTEGER
        DEFAULT 0,
    dia_diem VARCHAR(255)
        NOT NULL,
    hinh_thuc_chia_se VARCHAR(30)
        NOT NULL,
    hinh_thuc_trao_doi VARCHAR(30),
    trang_thai VARCHAR(30)
        DEFAULT 'KHA_DUNG',
    ngay_tao TIMESTAMPTZ
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    ngay_cap_nhat TIMESTAMPTZ
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT pk_bai_dang
        PRIMARY KEY(bai_dang_id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_bai_dang_nguoi_dung
        FOREIGN KEY(chu_so_huu_id)
        REFERENCES nguoi_dung(nguoi_dung_id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_bai_dang_danh_muc
        FOREIGN KEY(danh_muc_id)
        REFERENCES danh_muc_tai_san(danh_muc_id),
    CONSTRAINT ck_so_luong
        CHECK(
            so_luong_tong>=1
            AND so_luong_kha_dung>=0
            AND so_luong_giu_cho>=0
            AND so_luong_da_phan_phoi>=0
            AND
            so_luong_kha_dung
            +so_luong_giu_cho
            +so_luong_da_phan_phoi
            =so_luong_tong
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_hinh_thuc_chia_se
        CHECK(
            hinh_thuc_chia_se
            IN(
                'CHO_TANG',
                'TRAO_DOI'
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_hinh_thuc_trao_doi
        CHECK(
            (
                hinh_thuc_chia_se='CHO_TANG'
                AND hinh_thuc_trao_doi IS NULL
            )
            OR
            (
                hinh_thuc_chia_se='TRAO_DOI'
                AND hinh_thuc_trao_doi
                IN(
                    'TAI_SAN',
                    'TIEN'
                )
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_trang_thai_bai_dang
        CHECK(
            trang_thai
            IN(
                'KHA_DUNG',
                'TAM_HET_KHA_DUNG',
                'DA_KET_THUC'
            )
        )
);
4.6. B???ng hinh_anh_tai_san
CREATE TABLE hinh_anh_tai_san (
    hinh_anh_id UUID NOT NULL
        DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    bai_dang_id UUID NOT NULL,
    duong_dan_anh VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    thu_tu_hien_thi INTEGER NOT NULL
        DEFAULT 1,
    ngay_tai_len TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT pk_hinh_anh_tai_san
        PRIMARY KEY (hinh_anh_id),
    CONSTRAINT uq_hinh_anh_thu_tu
        UNIQUE (
            bai_dang_id,
            thu_tu_hien_thi
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_hinh_anh_duong_dan
        CHECK (
            CHAR_LENGTH(TRIM(duong_dan_anh)) > 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_hinh_anh_thu_tu
        CHECK (
            thu_tu_hien_thi >= 1
        ),
    CONSTRAINT fk_hinh_anh_bai_dang
        FOREIGN KEY (bai_dang_id)
        REFERENCES bai_dang_tai_san (bai_dang_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE CASCADE
);
4.7. B???ng de_xuat_giao_dich
CREATE TABLE de_xuat_giao_dich (
    de_xuat_id UUID NOT NULL
        DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    bai_dang_id UUID NOT NULL,
    nguoi_gui_id UUID NOT NULL,
    so_luong_yeu_cau INTEGER NOT NULL,
    loi_nhan TEXT,
    tai_san_doi_ung TEXT,
    tien_doi_ung NUMERIC(18,2),
    trang_thai VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL
        DEFAULT 'CHO_XU_LY',
    ly_do_tu_choi TEXT,
    ngay_gui TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    ngay_cap_nhat TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT pk_de_xuat_giao_dich
        PRIMARY KEY (de_xuat_id),
    CONSTRAINT ck_de_xuat_so_luong
        CHECK (
            so_luong_yeu_cau > 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_de_xuat_tien_doi_ung
        CHECK (
            tien_doi_ung IS NULL
            OR tien_doi_ung >= 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_de_xuat_loi_nhan
        CHECK (
            loi_nhan IS NULL
            OR CHAR_LENGTH(TRIM(loi_nhan)) > 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_de_xuat_tai_san_doi_ung
        CHECK (
            tai_san_doi_ung IS NULL
            OR CHAR_LENGTH(TRIM(tai_san_doi_ung)) > 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_de_xuat_trang_thai
        CHECK (
            trang_thai IN (
                'CHO_XU_LY',
                'DANG_THUONG_LUONG',
                'DA_CHAP_NHAN',
                'TU_CHOI',
                'DA_HUY',
                'HET_HIEU_LUC'
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_de_xuat_ly_do_tu_choi
        CHECK (
            trang_thai <> 'TU_CHOI'
            OR (
                ly_do_tu_choi IS NOT NULL
                AND CHAR_LENGTH(TRIM(ly_do_tu_choi)) > 0
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT fk_de_xuat_bai_dang
        FOREIGN KEY (bai_dang_id)
        REFERENCES bai_dang_tai_san (bai_dang_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT,
    CONSTRAINT fk_de_xuat_nguoi_gui
        FOREIGN KEY (nguoi_gui_id)
        REFERENCES nguoi_dung (nguoi_dung_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT
);
4.8. B???ng tin_nhan_thuong_luong
CREATE TABLE tin_nhan_thuong_luong (
    tin_nhan_id UUID NOT NULL
        DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    de_xuat_id UUID NOT NULL,
    nguoi_gui_id UUID NOT NULL,
    noi_dung TEXT NOT NULL,
    trang_thai VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL
        DEFAULT 'DA_GUI',
    thoi_gian_gui TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT pk_tin_nhan_thuong_luong
        PRIMARY KEY (tin_nhan_id),
    CONSTRAINT ck_tin_nhan_noi_dung
        CHECK (
            CHAR_LENGTH(TRIM(noi_dung)) > 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_tin_nhan_trang_thai
        CHECK (
            trang_thai IN (
                'DA_GUI',
                'DA_DOC',
                'BI_AN'
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT fk_tin_nhan_de_xuat
        FOREIGN KEY (de_xuat_id)
        REFERENCES de_xuat_giao_dich (de_xuat_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT,
    CONSTRAINT fk_tin_nhan_nguoi_gui
        FOREIGN KEY (nguoi_gui_id)
        REFERENCES nguoi_dung (nguoi_dung_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT
);
4.9. B???ng giao_dich
CREATE TABLE giao_dich (
    giao_dich_id UUID NOT NULL
        DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    de_xuat_id UUID NOT NULL,
    nguoi_so_huu_id UUID NOT NULL,
    nguoi_tiep_nhan_id UUID NOT NULL,
    so_luong_giao_dich INTEGER NOT NULL,
    thoi_gian_ban_giao TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    dia_diem_ban_giao VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    xac_nhan_nguoi_so_huu BOOLEAN NOT NULL
        DEFAULT FALSE,
    xac_nhan_nguoi_tiep_nhan BOOLEAN NOT NULL
        DEFAULT FALSE,
    ly_do_huy TEXT,
    trang_thai VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL
        DEFAULT 'CHO_BAN_GIAO',
    ngay_tao TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    ngay_cap_nhat TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT pk_giao_dich
        PRIMARY KEY (giao_dich_id),
    CONSTRAINT uq_giao_dich_de_xuat
        UNIQUE (de_xuat_id),
    CONSTRAINT ck_giao_dich_so_luong
        CHECK (
            so_luong_giao_dich > 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_giao_dich_hai_ben
        CHECK (
            nguoi_so_huu_id <> nguoi_tiep_nhan_id
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_giao_dich_dia_diem
        CHECK (
            CHAR_LENGTH(TRIM(dia_diem_ban_giao)) > 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_giao_dich_trang_thai
        CHECK (
            trang_thai IN (
                'CHO_BAN_GIAO',
                'CHO_BEN_CON_LAI_XAC_NHAN',
                'HOAN_TAT',
                'DA_HUY'
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_giao_dich_hoan_tat
        CHECK (
            trang_thai <> 'HOAN_TAT'
            OR (
                xac_nhan_nguoi_so_huu = TRUE
                AND xac_nhan_nguoi_tiep_nhan = TRUE
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_giao_dich_huy
        CHECK (
            trang_thai <> 'DA_HUY'
            OR (
                ly_do_huy IS NOT NULL
                AND CHAR_LENGTH(TRIM(ly_do_huy)) > 0
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT fk_giao_dich_de_xuat
        FOREIGN KEY (de_xuat_id)
        REFERENCES de_xuat_giao_dich (de_xuat_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT,
    CONSTRAINT fk_giao_dich_nguoi_so_huu
        FOREIGN KEY (nguoi_so_huu_id)
        REFERENCES nguoi_dung (nguoi_dung_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT,
    CONSTRAINT fk_giao_dich_nguoi_tiep_nhan
        FOREIGN KEY (nguoi_tiep_nhan_id)
        REFERENCES nguoi_dung (nguoi_dung_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT
);
4.10. B???ng danh_gia
CREATE TABLE danh_gia (
    danh_gia_id UUID NOT NULL
        DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    giao_dich_id UUID NOT NULL,
    nguoi_danh_gia_id UUID NOT NULL,
    nguoi_duoc_danh_gia_id UUID NOT NULL,
    diem_sao SMALLINT NOT NULL,
    nhan_xet TEXT,
    thoi_gian_danh_gia TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT pk_danh_gia
        PRIMARY KEY (danh_gia_id),
    CONSTRAINT uq_danh_gia_giao_dich_nguoi_danh_gia
        UNIQUE (
            giao_dich_id,
            nguoi_danh_gia_id
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_danh_gia_diem_sao
        CHECK (
            diem_sao BETWEEN 1 AND 5
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_danh_gia_hai_ben
        CHECK (
            nguoi_danh_gia_id <> nguoi_duoc_danh_gia_id
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_danh_gia_nhan_xet
        CHECK (
            nhan_xet IS NULL
            OR CHAR_LENGTH(TRIM(nhan_xet)) > 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT fk_danh_gia_giao_dich
        FOREIGN KEY (giao_dich_id)
        REFERENCES giao_dich (giao_dich_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT,
    CONSTRAINT fk_danh_gia_nguoi_danh_gia
        FOREIGN KEY (nguoi_danh_gia_id)
        REFERENCES nguoi_dung (nguoi_dung_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT,
    CONSTRAINT fk_danh_gia_nguoi_duoc_danh_gia
        FOREIGN KEY (nguoi_duoc_danh_gia_id)
        REFERENCES nguoi_dung (nguoi_dung_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT
);
4.11. B???ng bao_cao_vi_pham
CREATE TABLE bao_cao_vi_pham (
    bao_cao_id UUID NOT NULL
        DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    nguoi_bao_cao_id UUID NOT NULL,
    nguoi_dung_bi_bao_cao_id UUID,
    bai_dang_bi_bao_cao_id UUID,
    loai_bao_cao VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
    ly_do_vi_pham VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    mo_ta_chi_tiet TEXT NOT NULL,
    minh_chung VARCHAR(500),
    trang_thai_xu_ly VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL
        DEFAULT 'CHO_KIEM_DUYET',
    ngay_bao_cao TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    ngay_cap_nhat TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT pk_bao_cao_vi_pham
        PRIMARY KEY (bao_cao_id),
    CONSTRAINT ck_bao_cao_loai
        CHECK (
            loai_bao_cao IN (
                'NGUOI_DUNG',
                'BAI_DANG'
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_bao_cao_ly_do
        CHECK (
            CHAR_LENGTH(TRIM(ly_do_vi_pham)) > 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_bao_cao_noi_dung
        CHECK (
            CHAR_LENGTH(TRIM(mo_ta_chi_tiet)) > 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_bao_cao_minh_chung
        CHECK (
            minh_chung IS NULL
            OR CHAR_LENGTH(TRIM(minh_chung)) > 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_bao_cao_doi_tuong
        CHECK (
            (
                loai_bao_cao = 'NGUOI_DUNG'
                AND nguoi_dung_bi_bao_cao_id IS NOT NULL
                AND bai_dang_bi_bao_cao_id IS NULL
            )
            OR
            (
                loai_bao_cao = 'BAI_DANG'
                AND nguoi_dung_bi_bao_cao_id IS NULL
                AND bai_dang_bi_bao_cao_id IS NOT NULL
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_bao_cao_trang_thai
        CHECK (
            trang_thai_xu_ly IN (
                'CHO_KIEM_DUYET',
                'DANG_XU_LY',
                'CHO_BO_SUNG_MINH_CHUNG',
                'DA_XU_LY',
                'TU_CHOI',
                'KHONG_DU_CAN_CU'
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT fk_bao_cao_nguoi_gui
        FOREIGN KEY (nguoi_bao_cao_id)
        REFERENCES nguoi_dung (nguoi_dung_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT,
    CONSTRAINT fk_bao_cao_nguoi_bi_bao_cao
        FOREIGN KEY (nguoi_dung_bi_bao_cao_id)
        REFERENCES nguoi_dung (nguoi_dung_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT,
    CONSTRAINT fk_bao_cao_bai_dang
        FOREIGN KEY (bai_dang_bi_bao_cao_id)
        REFERENCES bai_dang_tai_san (bai_dang_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT
);
4.12. B???ng bien_phap_xu_ly
CREATE TABLE bien_phap_xu_ly (
    bien_phap_id UUID NOT NULL
        DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    bao_cao_id UUID NOT NULL,
    quan_tri_vien_id UUID NOT NULL,
    loai_bien_phap VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
    noi_dung_xu_ly TEXT NOT NULL,
    thoi_gian_xu_ly TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
        DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    CONSTRAINT pk_bien_phap_xu_ly
        PRIMARY KEY (bien_phap_id),
    CONSTRAINT ck_bien_phap_loai
        CHECK (
            loai_bien_phap IN (
                'CANH_BAO',
                'AN_BAI_DANG',
                'XOA_BAI_DANG',
                'KHOA_TAI_KHOAN',
                'KHONG_AP_DUNG_CHE_TAI'
            )
        ),
    CONSTRAINT ck_bien_phap_noi_dung
        CHECK (
            CHAR_LENGTH(TRIM(noi_dung_xu_ly)) > 0
        ),
    CONSTRAINT fk_bien_phap_bao_cao
        FOREIGN KEY (bao_cao_id)
        REFERENCES bao_cao_vi_pham (bao_cao_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT,
    CONSTRAINT fk_bien_phap_quan_tri_vien
        FOREIGN KEY (quan_tri_vien_id)
        REFERENCES nguoi_dung (nguoi_dung_id)
        ON UPDATE RESTRICT
        ON DELETE RESTRICT
);

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW vw_bai_dang_kha_dung AS
SELECT
    bd.bai_dang_id,
    bd.ten_tai_san,
    bd.mo_ta_hien_trang,
    bd.so_luong_tong,
    bd.so_luong_kha_dung,
    bd.dia_diem,
    bd.hinh_thuc_chia_se,
    bd.hinh_thuc_trao_doi,
    bd.danh_muc_id,
    dm.ten_danh_muc,
    bd.chu_so_huu_id,
    bd.ngay_tao
FROM bai_dang_tai_san bd

    ON dm.danh_muc_id = bd.danh_muc_id

  AND bd.so_luong_kha_dung > 0;
7.2. View h??? s?? uy t??n
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW vw_ho_so_uy_tin AS
SELECT
    nd.nguoi_dung_id,
    hs.ho_ten,
    hs.anh_dai_dien,
    hs.dia_chi,
    hs.mo_ta_ca_nhan,
    uy.diem_trung_binh,
    uy.tong_so_danh_gia,
    uy.so_giao_dich_hoan_tat,
    nd.trang_thai AS trang_thai_tai_khoan
FROM nguoi_dung nd
JOIN ho_so_thanh_vien hs
    ON hs.nguoi_dung_id = nd.nguoi_dung_id
JOIN ho_so_uy_tin uy
    ON uy.nguoi_dung_id = nd.nguoi_dung_id;
